<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1508_19fb9b-04 inner-column-1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading1508_be241e-96 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1508_be241e-96">Singapore For Everyone</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading1508_454bb4-da wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1508_454bb4-da"><strong>Locals’ Guide to Singapore Travel</strong></p>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity is-style-wide"/>



<div class="wp-block-group alignwide" style="padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--40);padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--80);padding-bottom:0;padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--80)"><div class="wp-block-group__inner-container is-layout-constrained wp-container-core-group-is-layout-f9c356e8 wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center" style="font-size:32px"><strong>Your best guide to&nbsp;</strong><mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-theme-palette-1-color">Singapore</mark><strong> from someone who lives here!</strong></h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center" style="font-size:24px">Are you visiting Singapore right now or planning a trip here?</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center" style="padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--60);font-size:24px">Don&#8217;t you wish you had a friend who lived here — someone who could give you the inside scoop on what to see, where to eat, shop, and more?</p>
</div></div>



<div class="aligncenter kt-sc1508_d5a485-df wp-block-kadence-splitcontent"><div class="kt-split-content-wrap kt-sc-media-side-left" style="grid-template-columns:40% auto"><div class="kt-sc-imgcol kt-sc-imgcol-bg-cover kt-sc-img-side-left"></div><div class="kt-sc-textcol kt-sc-text-valign-center kt-sc-text-halign-right"><div class="kt-sc-innter-col">
<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left" style="font-size:32px"><strong>If you answer </strong><mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-theme-palette-1-color">&#8220;yes!&#8221;</mark><strong> then this is the site for you.</strong></h2>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading" style="padding-right:0;font-size:26px">I live in Singapore, and I really know the city, on the ground.</h2>



<p style="font-size:26px"><mark style="background-color:#cce6f1" class="has-inline-color">I live it, eat it, shop it, and love it.</mark></p>



<p style="padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--20);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--40);font-size:24px">Daily, I learned the kinds of questions people have and what people want to know before and during their holiday in Singapore.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity is-style-wide"/>
</div></div></div></div>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id1508_b4f232-36 alignnone has-theme-palette8-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-layout-top-sep kt-row-sep-type-crv"><svg viewBox="0 0 1000 100" preserveAspectRatio="none"><path d="M1000,100c0,0 -270.987,-98 -500,-98c-229.013,0 -500,98 -500,98l1000,0Z" /></svg></div><div class="kt-row-layout-bottom-sep kt-row-sep-type-sltr"><svg viewBox="0 0 1000 100" preserveAspectRatio="none"><path d="M0,0l1000,100l-1000,0l0,-100Z" /></svg></div><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-left-golden kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1508_217161-3c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p class="has-text-align-center" style="padding-top:0;padding-right:0;padding-bottom:0;padding-left:0;font-size:28px">Hello!<br>Welcome, Everyone; I’m <mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-theme-palette-1-color"><strong>Gan.</strong></mark><br><br>I have lived in Singapore almost all of my life. <br>Today, I use my knowledge to help fellow travelers,&nbsp;<em>just like you,</em>&nbsp;explore Singapore like a pro. <br></p>
</div></div>
